       <div class="tab-pane fade in active" data-cname="explore_articles_links_newest" id="exploreNewestTab" role="tabpanel" test-id="explore_articles_links_newest">
        <div class="col" data-cname="explore_articles_links_newest" test-id="explore_articles_links_newest">
         <h6 class="first">
          <a data-cname="explore_articles_newest" href="/articles/masters_in_forensic_accounting_salary_jobs.html" test-id="explore_articles_newest">
           Masters in Forensic Accounting: Salary &amp; Jobs
          </a>
         </h6>
         <p>
          Do forensic accountants make good money? In this article, you'll find information about a forensic accountant's average salary for some sample career options.
         </p>
        </div>
